Decent small craft brewery. I really appreciated the recognition of service members this place has, for military, fire and police. The staff was super friendly, offering our kids some sodas. We were made to feel welcome. The beers were decent. A bit over flavored for my taste, but I‚Äôm starting to think that might be the OC style (think the Bruery with all their crazy flavors). I would come here again.</review>

This Starbucks is alright, definitely not my favorite in SCV. I do enjoy coming here to work and hang out though. The baristas are usually pretty friendly and accommodating.

There are usually quite a few people camping out at this Starbucks, either on their phones, laptops, or studying.

Since this Starbucks is in the plaza right next to Sierra Vista, it can get crowded and loud around the time the school gets out; as a lot of students like to come here to get a beverage with their friends.

Restroom here requires a code. This Starbucks is relatively clean, but it‚Äôs showing its age. Some of the circle tables are uneven and the outlets under the large table are placed upside down and loose so my MacBook charger always falls out.<//text>
